They have millions of uses in our society: they support us emotionally, they guide us, they help sniff things out. Arguably, there are no substitutes for what they provide for us. But it turns out that dogs don\'t see much difference between species, and they\'re as good-willed and helpful to other species as they are to humans. Tao, the 12-year-old golden retriever who had his eyes surgically removed due to glaucoma, and Oko, his trusty helper, are a testament to that.
Melanie Jackson, the loving owner of Tao, recounted how it all went. Last year, Tao got diagnosed with glaucoma, an eye disease where the eye can\'t effectively drain its fluids. The disease progressed unexpectedly and rapidly. One morning, Tao seemed to be doing just fine, but in the evening, he started shaking his head (dogs do that when they feel pain), and just a few hours later, he went blind in one eye and had the eye removed. In January, his other eye gave out and had to be removed as well.More info: Instagram"> <script type="text/javascript">

getSource: function(url) {
var _url = new URL(url);
var host = _url.hostname;
if (host === window.location.hostname && _url.searchParams.get('utm_campaign') && _url.searchParams.get('utm_source')) {
return [_url.searchParams.get('utm_campaign'), _url.searchParams.get('utm_source')];
}
return ['organic', host.substring(0, host.lastIndexOf('.')).replace('www.', '').replace('.co', '')];
},
convertSource: function(source) {
if (['fb', 'm.facebook', 'l.facebook'].indexOf(source) > -1) {
source = 'facebook';
} else if (source === 't') {
source = 'twitter';
} else if (source === 'googlem') {
source = 'google';
}
return source;
},
getMedium: function(source) {
var searchEngines = ['360', 'alice', 'alltheweb', 'altavista', 'aol', 'ask', 'auone', 'avg', 'babylon', 'baidu',
'biglobe', 'bing', 'centrum', 'comcast', 'conduit', 'cnn', 'daum', 'ekolay', 'eniro', 'globo', 'google',

'seznam', 'so', 'sogou', 'startsiden', 'szukacz', 'terra', 'tut', 'ukr', 'virgilio', 'voila', 'wirtulana',
'yahoo', 'yandex', 'yam'];
var socialPages = ['twitter', 'facebook', 'pinterest', 'linkedin', 'youtube'];
var medium = 'none';
if (searchEngines.indexOf(source) !== -1) {
medium = 'organic'
} else if (source.indexOf('mail.google') !== -1) {
medium = 'email';
} else if (socialPages.indexOf(source) !== -1) {
medium = 'social';
} else if (source.indexOf('boredpanda') === -1) {
medium = 'referral';
}
return medium;
},
updateUrl: function(source, medium, campaign) {
var url = new URL(window.location.href);
if (!url.searchParams.get('utm_campaign') && !url.searchParams.get('utm_source') && !url.searchParams.get('utm_medium')) {
url.searchParams.set('utm_source', source);
url.searchParams.set('utm_medium', medium);
url.searchParams.set('utm_campaign', campaign);
if (history.replaceState) {
window.history.replaceState({path: url.toString()}, '', url.toString());
}
}
}

They have millions of uses in our society: they support us emotionally, they guide us, they help sniff things out. Arguably, there are no substitutes for what they provide for us. But it turns out that dogs don&rsquo;t see much difference between species, and they&rsquo;re as good-willed and helpful to other species as they are to humans. Tao, the 12-year-old golden retriever who had his eyes surgically removed due to glaucoma, and Oko, his trusty helper, are a testament to that.</p><div class="post-mobile-ad-within-content in-content-margin visible-upto-xs post-ads"><div class="dfp-ad"><div id="div-gpt-ad-1491844559200-0"><script type="text/javascript">
if (BoredPanda.Config.isMobileWidth) {
googletag.cmd.push(function() {
googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-1491844559200-0');
});
}</script></div><div id="BPM01_Mobile_300x250"></div></div></div><p>Melanie Jackson, the loving owner of Tao, recounted how it all went. Last year, Tao got diagnosed with glaucoma, an eye disease where the eye can&rsquo;t effectively drain its fluids. The disease progressed unexpectedly and rapidly. One morning, Tao seemed to be doing just fine, but in the evening, he started shaking his head (dogs do that when they feel pain), and just a few hours later, he went blind in one eye and had the eye removed. In January, his other eye gave out and had to be removed as well.</p><p class="post-content-source">More info: <a href="https://www.instagram.com/tao_mr_winky/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a></p><h2>Tao got diagnosed with glaucoma and lost both of his eyes. Despite his blindness, he recovered quickly and was happy again</h2><div class="shareable-post-image"><p class="attachment-link-container shareable-image-block" id="Know-the-history-of-this-adorable-dog-that-became-the-guide-animal-of-a-puppy-that-went-totally-blind-5f76d59387083__880" data-href="http://www.boredpanda.com/animals-guide-puppy-leads-blind-dog-tao-oko-mr-winky/?image_id=Know-the-history-of-this-adorable-dog-that-became-the-guide-animal-of-a-puppy-that-went-totally-blind-5f76d59387083__880.jpg"><img src="https://static.boredpanda.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Know-the-history-of-this-adorable-dog-that-became-the-guide-animal-of-a-puppy-that-went-totally-blind-5f76d59387083__880.jpg" width="880" height="880"><span class="image-share-box"> <a href="javascript:void(0);" class="fb-share social-button" onclick=" var description = ''; if ($('meta[property=\'og:description\']').length &gt; 0) { description = $('meta[property=\'og:description\']').attr('content'); } window.open('https://www.facebook.com/dialog/feed?display=popup&amp;\

function placeholderImages(){
function imgLoaded(){
this.style.height = null;
this.removeEventListener('load', imgLoaded);
this.removeEventListener('error', imgLoaded);
}
var images = document.images;
for(var i = 0; i < images.length; i++){
var img = images[i];
if(img.complete) continue;
var height = img.getAttribute('height'), width = img.getAttribute('width');
if(height && width) {
img.style.height = height * img.clientWidth/width + 'px';
img.addEventListener('load', imgLoaded);
img.addEventListener('error', imgLoaded);
}
}
}
placeholderImages();

BoredPanda.TrafficSources = {
init: function() {
var source = '';
var medium = '';
var campaign = '';
if (document.referrer) {

[campaign, source] = this.getSource(referrer);
source = this.convertSource(source);
medium = this.getMedium(source);
if (source.indexOf('boredpanda') === -1 && !(source === 'trending' && campaign === 'sidebar')) {
this.updateUrl(source, medium, campaign)
}
}
},
getSource: function(url) {
var _url = new URL(url);
var host = _url.hostname;
if (host === window.location.hostname && _url.searchParams.get('utm_campaign') && _url.searchParams.get('utm_source')) {
return [_url.searchParams.get('utm_campaign'), _url.searchParams.get('utm_source')];
}
return ['organic', host.substring(0, host.lastIndexOf('.')).replace('www.', '').replace('.co', '')];
},
convertSource: function(source) {
if (['fb', 'm.facebook', 'l.facebook'].indexOf(source) > -1) {
source = 'facebook';
} else if (source === 't') {
source = 'twitter';
} else if (source === 'googlem') {
source = 'google';
}
return source;
},
getMedium: function(source) {
var searchEngines = ['360', 'alice', 'alltheweb', 'altavista', 'aol', 'ask', 'auone', 'avg', 'babylon', 'baidu',
'biglobe', 'bing', 'centrum', 'comcast', 'conduit', 'cnn', 'daum', 'ekolay', 'eniro', 'globo', 'google',
'haosou', 'incredimail', 'kvasir', 'live', 'lycos', 'lycos', 'other', 'mamma', 'msn', 'mynet', 'najdi', 'naver',
'netscape', 'onet', 'ozu', 'pchome', 'rakuten', 'rambler', 'search-results', 'search.smt.docomo', 'sesam',
'seznam', 'so', 'sogou', 'startsiden', 'szukacz', 'terra', 'tut', 'ukr', 'virgilio', 'voila', 'wirtulana',
'yahoo', 'yandex', 'yam'];
var socialPages = ['twitter', 'facebook', 'pinterest', 'linkedin', 'youtube'];
var medium = 'none';
if (searchEngines.indexOf(source) !== -1) {
medium = 'organic'
} else if (source.indexOf('mail.google') !== -1) {
medium = 'email';
} else if (socialPages.indexOf(source) !== -1) {
medium = 'social';
} else if (source.indexOf('boredpanda') === -1) {
medium = 'referral';
}
return medium;
},
updateUrl: function(source, medium, campaign) {
var url = new URL(window.location.href);
if (!url.searchParams.get('utm_campaign') && !url.searchParams.get('utm_source') && !url.searchParams.get('utm_medium')) {
url.searchParams.set('utm_source', source);
url.searchParams.set('utm_medium', medium);
url.searchParams.set('utm_campaign', campaign);
if (history.replaceState) {
window.history.replaceState({path: url.toString()}, '', url.toString());
}
}
}
};

But it turns out that dogs don't see much difference between species, and they're as good-willed and helpful to other species as they are to humans. Tao, the 12-year-old golden retriever who had his eyes surgically removed due to glaucoma, and Oko, his trusty helper, are a testament to that.","articleBody":"Melanie Jackson, the loving owner of Tao, recounted how it all went. Last year, Tao got diagnosed with glaucoma, an eye disease where the eye can't effectively drain its fluids. The disease progressed unexpectedly and rapidly. One morning, Tao seemed to be doing just fine, but in the evening, he started shaking his head (dogs do that when they feel pain), and just a few hours later, he went blind in one eye and had the eye removed. In January, his other eye gave out and had to be removed as well. }</script></div><div id="BP02_300x250_InArticle"></div></div> </div> <p>Dogs are very helpful to us, humans. They have millions of uses in our society: they support us emotionally, they guide us, they help sniff things out. Arguably, there are no substitutes for what they provide for us. But it turns out that dogs don&rsquo;t see much difference between species, and they&rsquo;re as good-willed and helpful to other species as they are to humans. Tao, the 12-year-old golden retriever who had his eyes surgically removed due to glaucoma, and Oko, his trusty helper, are a testament to that.</p><div class="post-mobile-ad-within-content in-content-margin visible-upto-xs post-ads"><div class="dfp-ad"><div id="div-gpt-ad-1491844559200-0"><script type="text/javascript">
if (BoredPanda.Config.isMobileWidth) {
googletag.cmd.push(function() {

});
}</script></div><div id="BPM01_Mobile_300x250"></div></div></div><p>Melanie Jackson, the loving owner of Tao, recounted how it all went. Last year, Tao got diagnosed with glaucoma, an eye disease where the eye can&rsquo;t effectively drain its fluids. The disease progressed unexpectedly and rapidly. One morning, Tao seemed to be doing just fine, but in the evening, he started shaking his head (dogs do that when they feel pain), and just a few hours later, he went blind in one eye and had the eye removed. In January, his other eye gave out and had to be removed as well.</p><p class="post-content-source">More info: <a href="https://www.instagram.com/tao_mr_winky/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a></p><h2>Tao got diagnosed with glaucoma and lost both of his eyes. function placeholderImages(){
function imgLoaded(){
this.style.height = null;
this.removeEventListener('load', imgLoaded);
this.removeEventListener('error', imgLoaded);
}
var images = document.images;
for(var i = 0; i < images.length; i++){
var img = images[i];
if(img.complete) continue;
var height = img.getAttribute('height'), width = img.getAttribute('width');
if(height && width) {
img.style.height = height * img.clientWidth/width + 'px';
img.addEventListener('load', imgLoaded);
img.addEventListener('error', imgLoaded);
}
}
}
placeholderImages();
</script> <script type="text/javascript">

function create_UUID() {
var dt = new Date().getTime();
var uuid = 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function(c) {
var r = (dt + Math.random()*16)%16 | 0;
dt = Math.floor(dt/16);
return (c=='x' ? r :(r&0x3|0x8)).toString(16);
});
return uuid;
}
